━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/editor/editor_operations.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Editor Operations Module
// Handles Monaco editor operations including open, close, and save

async function openEditor(panel, file) {
    try {
        let content = '';
        if (panel === 'local') {
            content = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/read?path=${encodeURIComponent(state.local.currentPath + '/' + file.name)}`).then(r => r.text());
        } else {
            const data = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/read?path=${encodeURIComponent(file.path || file.name)}`).then(r => r.json());
            content = data.content;
        }
        
        state.editor.currentFile = { panel, file, originalContent: content };
        state.editor.visible = true;
        state.editor.modified = false;
        
        document.getElementById('editor-filename').textContent = file.name;
        document.getElementById('editor-dirty').classList.add('hidden');
        
        document.getElementById('left-panel').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('right-panel').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('resizer-1').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('main-header').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('mode-indicator').style.display = 'none';
        
        const editorPanel = document.getElementById('editor-panel');
        editorPanel.style.width = '100%';
        editorPanel.classList.add('active');
        
        if (state.editorInstance) {
            const lang = getLanguage(file.name);
            state.monaco.editor.setModelLanguage(state.editorInstance.getModel(), lang);
            state.editorInstance.setValue(content);
            document.getElementById('editor-lang').textContent = lang;
        }
    } catch (error) {
        showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    }
}

function closeEditor() {
    if (state.editor.modified && !confirm('Discard changes?')) return;
    
    state.editor.visible = false;
    state.editor.currentFile = null;
    state.editor.modified = false;
    
    closeDropdownLocal();
    closeDropdownGithub();
    
    document.getElementById('editor-panel').classList.remove('active');
    
    document.getElementById('left-panel').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('right-panel').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('resizer-1').style.display = 'block';
    document.getElementById('main-header').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('mode-indicator').style.display = 'flex';
}

function toggleEditor() {
    if (state.editor.visible) closeEditor();
    else if (state.editor.currentFile) openEditor(state.editor.currentFile.panel, state.editor.currentFile.file);
}

async function saveCurrentFile() {
    if (!state.editor.currentFile) return;
    
    const { panel, file } = state.editor.currentFile;
    const content = state.editorInstance.getValue();
    
    try {
        if (panel === 'local') {
            await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/write`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ path: state.local.currentPath + '/' + file.name, content })
            });
        } else {
            await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/update`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ 
                    path: file.path || file.name, 
                    content, 
                    sha: file.sha 
                })
            });
            await loadGitHubFiles(state.github.currentPath);
        }
        
        state.editor.modified = false;
        document.getElementById('editor-dirty').classList.add('hidden');
        showNotification('Saved', 'success');
    } catch (error) {
        showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    }
}

// Export functions globally
window.openEditor = openEditor;
window.closeEditor = closeEditor;
window.toggleEditor = toggleEditor;
window.saveCurrentFile = saveCurrentFile;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Monaco Editor Initializer Module
// Handles initialization of the Monaco code editor

function initMonaco() {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
        require.config({ paths: { 'vs': 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/monaco-editor/0.45.0/min/vs' }});
        require(['vs/editor/editor.main'], function() {
            state.monaco = monaco;
            state.editorInstance = monaco.editor.create(document.getElementById('monaco-container'), {
                value: '',
                language: 'plaintext',
                theme: 'vs-dark',
                automaticLayout: true,
                minimap: { enabled: false },
                fontSize: 14,
                fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono',
                scrollBeyondLastLine: false,
                roundedSelection: false,
                padding: { top: 16 },
                quickSuggestions: false,
                suggestOnTriggerCharacters: false,
                acceptSuggestionOnEnter: 'off',
                tabCompletion: 'off',
                wordBasedSuggestions: false,
                parameterHints: { enabled: false },
                hover: { enabled: false },
                formatOnType: false,
                autoIndent: 'none',
                dragAndDrop: false
            });
            
            state.editorInstance.onDidChangeCursorPosition((e) => {
                document.getElementById('editor-cursor').textContent = `Ln ${e.position.lineNumber}, Col ${e.position.column}`;
            });
            
            state.editorInstance.onDidChangeModelContent(() => {
                if (!state.editor.modified && state.editor.currentFile) {
                    state.editor.modified = true;
                    document.getElementById('editor-dirty').classList.remove('hidden');
                }
            });
            
            resolve();
        });
    });
}

// Export function globally
window.initMonaco = initMonaco;

// Main Application Loader
// Loads all modules in the correct dependency order

// Module loading order is critical for dependencies
const MODULES = [
    // 1. State (must be first - provides global state)
    'state/app_state.js',
    
    // 2. Utilities (no dependencies)
    'utils/file_utils.js',
    
    // 3. UI Systems (depends on state)
    'ui/notification_system.js',
    'ui/app_styles.css',
    
    // 4. Services (depends on state, utils, notifications)
    'services/server_health.js',
    'services/file_loader.js',
    
    // 5. Renderers (depends on state, utils, services)
    'renderers/file_list_renderer.js',
    
    // 6. Handlers (depends on state, renderers, services)
    'handlers/touch_handlers.js',
    'handlers/resizer_dragdrop.js',
    'handlers/keyboard_shortcuts.js',
    
    // 7. Features (depends on most other modules)
    'features/selection_system.js',
    'features/batch_operations.js',
    'features/inline_operations.js',
    'features/tree_view.js',
    'features/search_system.js',
    'features/panel_mode_manager.js',
    
    // 8. UI Components (depends on features)
    'ui/context_menu.js',
    'ui/properties_panel.js',
    'ui/dropdown_manager.js',
    'ui/breadcrumb_manager.js',
    
    // 9. GitHub Integration (depends on state, services, ui)
    'github/github_connection.js',
    
    // 10. Transfer Operations (depends on state, ui, services)
    'transfer/transfer_operations.js',
    
    // 11. Editor (depends on state, services, ui)
    'editor/monaco_initializer.js',
    'editor/editor_operations.js',
    
    // 12. Event Listeners (must be last - wires everything together)
    'handlers/event_listeners.js'
];

// Base path for modules
const MODULE_BASE_PATH = 'index/modules/';

// Load a single script module
function loadScript(src) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        const script = document.createElement('script');
        script.src = MODULE_BASE_PATH + src;
        script.type = 'text/javascript';
        script.onload = () => resolve(src);
        script.onerror = () => reject(new Error(`Failed to load: ${src}`));
        document.head.appendChild(script);
    });
}

// Load CSS (just for tracking - CSS is loaded via link tag in HTML)
function loadCSS(src) {
    return Promise.resolve(src); // CSS is loaded via link tag
}

// Load all modules in sequence
async function loadAllModules() {
    console.log('[AppLoader] Starting module loading...');
    
    for (const module of MODULES) {
        if (module.endsWith('.css')) {
            // CSS is already loaded via link tag
            console.log(`[AppLoader] CSS already loaded: ${module}`);
        } else {
            try {
                await loadScript(module);
                console.log(`[AppLoader] Loaded: ${module}`);
            } catch (error) {
                console.error(`[AppLoader] Failed to load: ${module}`, error);
                throw error;
            }
        }
    }
    
    console.log('[AppLoader] All modules loaded successfully');
}

// Initialize the application after modules are loaded
async function initializeApplication() {
    await loadAllModules();
    
    // Now that all modules are loaded, initialize the app
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        initMonaco().then(() => {
            setupEventListeners();
            setupResizers();
            setupGlobalTouchHandlers();
            setupKeyboardShortcuts();
            checkServerHealth().then(() => {
                loadLocalFiles(state.local.currentPath);
                if (state.github.token && state.github.repo) {
                    document.getElementById('gh-token').value = state.github.token;
                    document.getElementById('gh-repo').value = state.github.repo;
                    connectGitHub(true);
                }
            });
        });
    });
}

// Start loading modules
initializeApplication();

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Batch Operations Module
// Handles batch transfer, delete, and properties operations

async function batchTransfer() {
    const sourcePanel = state.local.selectedFiles.size > 0 ? 'local' : 'github';
    const targetPanel = sourcePanel === 'local' ? 'github' : 'local';
    const panelState = sourcePanel === 'local' ? state.local : state.github;
    
    const files = Array.from(panelState.selectedFiles).map(name => {
        return panelState.files.find(f => f.name === name);
    }).filter(Boolean);
    
    if (files.length === 0) return;
    
    const progressModal = document.getElementById('batch-progress-modal');
    const progressText = document.getElementById('batch-progress-text');
    const progressCount = document.getElementById('batch-progress-count');
    const progressFill = document.getElementById('batch-progress-fill');
    
    progressModal.classList.add('active');
    progressText.textContent = `Transferring ${files.length} files...`;
    
    const operations = files.map(file => ({
        direction: sourcePanel === 'local' ? 'local-to-github' : 'github-to-local',
        source: sourcePanel === 'local' 
            ? `${state.local.currentPath}/${file.name}`
            : (file.path || file.name),
        destination: sourcePanel === 'local'
            ? `${state.github.currentPath ? state.github.currentPath + '/' : ''}${file.name}`
            : `${state.local.currentPath}/${file.name}`,
        message: `Batch transfer ${file.name}`
    }));
    
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/transfer/batch`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ operations })
        });
        
        const result = await response.json();
        
        for (let i = 0; i <= files.length; i++) {
            progressCount.textContent = `${i}/${files.length}`;
            progressFill.style.width = `${(i / files.length) * 100}%`;
            await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 100));
        }
        
        progressModal.classList.remove('active');
        
        if (result.success) {
            showNotification(`Transferred ${result.completed} files`, 'success');
        } else {
            showNotification(`Completed with ${result.errors.length} errors`, 'warning');
        }
        
        clearSelection();
        refreshPanel(targetPanel);
    } catch (error) {
        progressModal.classList.remove('active');
        showNotification(`Transfer failed: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    }
}

async function batchDelete() {
    const panel = state.local.selectedFiles.size > 0 ? 'local' : 'github';
    const panelState = panel === 'local' ? state.local : state.github;
    
    const files = Array.from(panelState.selectedFiles).map(name => {
        return panelState.files.find(f => f.name === name);
    }).filter(Boolean);
    
    if (files.length === 0) return;
    
    if (!confirm(`Delete ${files.length} items?`)) return;
    
    let successCount = 0;
    let errorCount = 0;
    
    for (const file of files) {
        try {
            if (panel === 'local') {
                await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/delete`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ path: `${state.local.currentPath}/${file.name}` })
                });
            } else {
                await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/delete`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ 
                        path: file.path || file.name, 
                        sha: file.sha, 
                        message: `Delete ${file.name}` 
                    })
                });
            }
            successCount++;
        } catch (err) {
            errorCount++;
        }
    }
    
    showNotification(`Deleted ${successCount} items${errorCount > 0 ? `, ${errorCount} failed` : ''}`, successCount > 0 ? 'success' : 'error');
    clearSelection();
    refreshPanel(panel);
}

function batchProperties() {
    const panel = state.local.selectedFiles.size > 0 ? 'local' : 'github';
    const panelState = panel === 'local' ? state.local : state.github;
    
    const files = Array.from(panelState.selectedFiles).map(name => {
        return panelState.files.find(f => f.name === name);
    }).filter(Boolean);
    
    showProperties(panel, files[0], true);
}

// Export functions globally
window.batchTransfer = batchTransfer;
window.batchDelete = batchDelete;
window.batchProperties = batchProperties;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Panel Mode Manager Module
// Handles panel mode switching and swapping

function setPanelMode(left, right) {
    state.panelMode.left = left;
    state.panelMode.right = right;
    updateModeIndicator();
    refreshPanel('local');
    refreshPanel('github');
}

function swapPanels() {
    const temp = state.panelMode.left;
    state.panelMode.left = state.panelMode.right;
    state.panelMode.right = temp;
    updateModeIndicator();
    refreshPanel('local');
    refreshPanel('github');
}

function updateModeIndicator() {
    const leftChar = state.panelMode.left === 'storage' ? 'S' : 'G';
    const rightChar = state.panelMode.right === 'storage' ? 'S' : 'G';
    document.getElementById('mode-text').textContent = `${leftChar} | ${rightChar}`;
    
    // Update panel titles
    document.getElementById('left-panel-title').textContent = state.panelMode.left === 'storage' ? 'Device' : 'GitHub';
    document.getElementById('right-panel-title').textContent = state.panelMode.right === 'storage' ? 'Device' : 'GitHub';
    
    // Update header colors
    const leftHeader = document.querySelector('#left-panel .panel-header div');
    const rightHeader = document.querySelector('#right-panel .panel-header div');
    
    if (state.panelMode.left === 'storage') {
        leftHeader.className = 'flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-medium text-blue-400 flex-1 min-w-0';
        leftHeader.innerHTML = '<button id="btn-local-back" class="back-btn touch-btn"><i class="fas fa-arrow-left"></i></button><i class="fas fa-mobile-alt"></i><span class="truncate" id="left-panel-title">Device</span>';
    } else {
        leftHeader.className = 'flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-medium text-green-400 flex-1 min-w-0';
        leftHeader.innerHTML = '<button id="btn-github-back" class="back-btn touch-btn"><i class="fas fa-arrow-left"></i></button><i class="fab fa-github"></i><span class="truncate" id="left-panel-title">GitHub</span>';
    }
    
    if (state.panelMode.right === 'storage') {
        rightHeader.className = 'flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-medium text-blue-400 flex-1 min-w-0';
        rightHeader.innerHTML = '<button id="btn-github-back" class="back-btn touch-btn"><i class="fas fa-arrow-left"></i></button><i class="fas fa-mobile-alt"></i><span class="truncate" id="right-panel-title">Device</span>';
    } else {
        rightHeader.className = 'flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-medium text-green-400 flex-1 min-w-0';
        rightHeader.innerHTML = '<button id="btn-github-back" class="back-btn touch-btn"><i class="fas fa-arrow-left"></i></button><i class="fab fa-github"></i><span class="truncate" id="right-panel-title">GitHub</span>';
    }
    
    // Re-attach event listeners
    document.getElementById('btn-local-back').addEventListener('click', () => navigateUp('local'));
    document.getElementById('btn-github-back').addEventListener('click', () => navigateUp('github'));
}

// Export functions globally
window.setPanelMode = setPanelMode;
window.swapPanels = swapPanels;
window.updateModeIndicator = updateModeIndicator;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/features/inline_operations.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Inline Operations Module
// Handles inline folder creation and file renaming

function createFolderInline(panel) {
    const container = document.getElementById(`${panel}-files`);
    
    // Check if already creating
    if (container.querySelector('.inline-input-row')) return;
    
    const inlineRow = document.createElement('div');
    inlineRow.className = 'inline-input-row';
    inlineRow.innerHTML = `
        <i class="fas fa-folder text-yellow-500"></i>
        <input type="text" class="inline-input" placeholder="Folder name..." autofocus>
        <button class="inline-btn cancel"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button>
        <button class="inline-btn confirm"><i class="fas fa-check"></i></button>
    `;
    
    container.insertBefore(inlineRow, container.firstChild);
    
    const input = inlineRow.querySelector('.inline-input');
    const cancelBtn = inlineRow.querySelector('.cancel');
    const confirmBtn = inlineRow.querySelector('.confirm');
    
    input.focus();
    
    cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', () => inlineRow.remove());
    
    confirmBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        const name = input.value.trim();
        if (!name) {
            inlineRow.remove();
            return;
        }
        
        try {
            if (panel === 'local') {
                await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/mkdir`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ path: `${state.local.currentPath}/${name}` })
                });
            } else {
                await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/create`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ 
                        path: `${state.github.currentPath ? state.github.currentPath + '/' : ''}${name}/.gitkeep`, 
                        content: '' 
                    })
                });
            }
            
            inlineRow.remove();
            showNotification('Folder created', 'success');
            refreshPanel(panel);
        } catch (error) {
            showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
        }
    });
    
    input.addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
        if (e.key === 'Enter') confirmBtn.click();
        if (e.key === 'Escape') cancelBtn.click();
    });
    
    input.addEventListener('blur', () => {
        setTimeout(() => {
            if (!inlineRow.contains(document.activeElement)) {
                inlineRow.remove();
            }
        }, 200);
    });
}

function renameInline(panel, file) {
    const container = document.getElementById(`${panel}-files`);
    const items = container.querySelectorAll('.file-item');
    let targetItem = null;
    
    items.forEach(item => {
        if (item.dataset.name === file.name) {
            targetItem = item;
        }
    });
    
    if (!targetItem) return;
    
    const originalContent = targetItem.innerHTML;
    const originalName = file.name;
    
    targetItem.innerHTML = `
        <div class="inline-input-row w-full">
            <i class="${getFileIcon(file.name, file.type)} ${file.type === 'directory' ? 'text-yellow-500' : 'text-blue-400'}"></i>
            <input type="text" class="inline-input" value="${file.name}" autofocus>
            <button class="inline-btn cancel"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button>
            <button class="inline-btn confirm"><i class="fas fa-check"></i></button>
        </div>
    `;
    
    const input = targetItem.querySelector('.inline-input');
    const cancelBtn = targetItem.querySelector('.cancel');
    const confirmBtn = targetItem.querySelector('.confirm');
    
    input.focus();
    input.select();
    
    const cancelRename = () => {
        targetItem.innerHTML = originalContent;
        const fileData = panel === 'local' 
            ? state.local.files.find(f => f.name === originalName)
            : state.github.files.find(f => f.name === originalName);
        if (fileData) {
            attachTouchHandlers(targetItem, panel, fileData, 0);
        }
    };
    
    cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', cancelRename);
    
    confirmBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        const newName = input.value.trim();
        if (!newName || newName === originalName) {
            cancelRename();
            return;
        }
        
        try {
            if (panel === 'local') {
                await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/rename`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ 
                        oldPath: `${state.local.currentPath}/${originalName}`,
                        newPath: `${state.local.currentPath}/${newName}`
                    })
                });
            } else {
                await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/rename`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ 
                        oldPath: file.path || originalName,
                        newPath: `${state.github.currentPath ? state.github.currentPath + '/' : ''}${newName}`,
                        sha: file.sha,
                        message: `Rename ${originalName} to ${newName}`
                    })
                });
            }
            
            showNotification('Renamed successfully', 'success');
            refreshPanel(panel);
        } catch (error) {
            showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
            cancelRename();
        }
    });
    
    input.addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
        if (e.key === 'Enter') confirmBtn.click();
        if (e.key === 'Escape') cancelRename();
    });
}

// Export functions globally
window.createFolderInline = createFolderInline;
window.renameInline = renameInline;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/features/tree_view.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Tree View Module
// Handles displaying directory tree structure

async function showTreeView(panel, file) {
    if (file.type !== 'directory') {
        showNotification('Tree view only available for directories', 'warning');
        return;
    }
    
    const modal = document.getElementById('tree-modal');
    const title = document.getElementById('tree-title');
    const content = document.getElementById('tree-content');
    
    title.textContent = `Tree: ${file.name}`;
    content.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center p-4"><div class="spinner inline-block"></div><p class="mt-2 text-gray-400">Loading...</p></div>';
    modal.classList.remove('hidden');
    modal.classList.add('flex');
    
    try {
        const path = panel === 'local' 
            ? `${state.local.currentPath}/${file.name}`
            : (file.path || file.name);
        
        if (panel === 'local') {
            const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/tree?path=${encodeURIComponent(path)}`);
            const data = await response.json();
            
            if (data.success) {
                content.innerHTML = `<pre class="tree-view">${renderTree(data.tree, '')}</pre>`;
            }
        } else {
            content.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center p-4 text-gray-400">Tree view for GitHub directories coming soon</div>';
        }
    } catch (err) {
        content.innerHTML = `<div class="text-center p-4 text-red-400">Error loading tree: ${err.message}</div>`;
    }
}

function renderTree(items, prefix) {
    if (!items || items.length === 0) return '';
    
    let result = '';
    items.forEach((item, index) => {
        const isLast = index === items.length - 1;
        const connector = isLast ? '└── ' : '├── ';
        const childPrefix = prefix + (isLast ? '    ' : '│   ');
        
        result += prefix + connector + item.name + '\n';
        
        if (item.children && item.children.length > 0) {
            result += renderTree(item.children, childPrefix);
        }
    });
    
    return result;
}

function closeTreeModal() {
    const modal = document.getElementById('tree-modal');
    modal.classList.add('hidden');
    modal.classList.remove('flex');
}

function copyTreeToClipboard() {
    const content = document.getElementById('tree-content').textContent;
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(content).then(() => {
        showNotification('Tree copied to clipboard', 'success');
    });
}

// Export functions globally
window.showTreeView = showTreeView;
window.renderTree = renderTree;
window.closeTreeModal = closeTreeModal;
window.copyTreeToClipboard = copyTreeToClipboard;

FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/features/selection_system.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Selection System Module
// Handles multi-select functionality and selection UI updates

function toggleFileSelection(panel, fileName) {
    const panelState = panel === 'local' ? state.local : state.github;
    
    if (panelState.selectedFiles.has(fileName)) {
        panelState.selectedFiles.delete(fileName);
    } else {
        panelState.selectedFiles.add(fileName);
    }
    
    updateSelectionUI(panel);
}

function updateSelectionUI(panel) {
    const panelState = panel === 'local' ? state.local : state.github;
    const container = document.getElementById(`${panel}-files`);
    const items = container.querySelectorAll('.file-item');
    
    items.forEach(item => {
        const name = item.dataset.name;
        if (panelState.selectedFiles.has(name)) {
            item.classList.add('selected');
        } else {
            item.classList.remove('selected');
        }
    });
    
    const selectionBar = document.getElementById('selection-bar');
    const selectionCount = document.getElementById('selection-count');
    
    if (panelState.selectedFiles.size > 0) {
        panelState.selectionMode = true;
        selectionBar.classList.add('active');
        selectionCount.textContent = `${panelState.selectedFiles.size} selected`;
    } else {
        panelState.selectionMode = false;
        selectionBar.classList.remove('active');
    }
}

function clearSelection() {
    state.local.selectedFiles.clear();
    state.local.selectionMode = false;
    state.github.selectedFiles.clear();
    state.github.selectionMode = false;
    
    document.querySelectorAll('.file-item.selected').forEach(item => {
        item.classList.remove('selected');
    });
    
    document.getElementById('selection-bar').classList.remove('active');
}

// Export functions globally
window.toggleFileSelection = toggleFileSelection;
window.updateSelectionUI = updateSelectionUI;
window.clearSelection = clearSelection;

FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/features/search_system.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Search System Module
// Handles search functionality for files

function toggleSearch(panel) {
    const searchBox = document.getElementById('search-box');
    const searchInput = document.getElementById('search-input');
    
    state.searchActive = !state.searchActive;
    state.searchPanel = panel;
    
    if (state.searchActive) {
        searchBox.classList.add('active');
        searchInput.focus();
    } else {
        searchBox.classList.remove('active');
        searchInput.value = '';
        // Clear filter
        if (panel === 'local' || (panel === 'left' && state.panelMode.left === 'storage') || (panel === 'right' && state.panelMode.right === 'storage')) {
            renderFileList('local', state.local.files);
        } else {
            renderFileList('github', state.github.files);
        }
    }
}

function handleSearch(e) {
    const query = e.target.value.toLowerCase().trim();
    if (!query) {
        renderFileList('local', state.local.files);
        renderFileList('github', state.github.files);
        return;
    }
    
    // Parse search query
    const isPattern = query.includes('*') || query.includes('?');
    const isSizeQuery = query.startsWith('size>');
    const isModifiedQuery = query.startsWith('modified:');
    const isNameQuery = query.startsWith('name:');
    
    // Filter local files
    const filteredLocal = state.local.files.filter(file => {
        if (isPattern) {
            const pattern = query.replace(/\*/g, '.*').replace(/\?/g, '.');
            return new RegExp(pattern, 'i').test(file.name);
        }
        if (isNameQuery) {
            const nameValue = query.replace('name:', '').trim();
            return file.name.toLowerCase().includes(nameValue);
        }
        return file.name.toLowerCase().includes(query);
    });
    
    // Filter GitHub files
    const filteredGithub = state.github.files.filter(file => {
        if (isPattern) {
            const pattern = query.replace(/\*/g, '.*').replace(/\?/g, '.');
            return new RegExp(pattern, 'i').test(file.name);
        }
        return file.name.toLowerCase().includes(query);
    });
    
    renderFileList('local', filteredLocal);
    renderFileList('github', filteredGithub);
}

// Export functions globally
window.toggleSearch = toggleSearch;
window.handleSearch = handleSearch;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// GitHub Connection Module
// Handles GitHub authentication and connection

function showGitHubConfig() {
    document.getElementById('github-config').classList.toggle('hidden');
}

async function connectGitHub(silent = false) {
    const token = document.getElementById('gh-token').value;
    const repo = document.getElementById('gh-repo').value;
    
    if (!token || !repo) {
        if (!silent) showNotification('Enter token and repo', 'error');
        return;
    }
    
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/connect`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ token, repo })
        });
        
        const data = await response.json();
        
        if (data.success) {
            state.github.connected = true;
            state.github.token = token;
            state.github.repo = repo;
            state.github.branch = data.branch || 'main';
            localStorage.setItem('gh_token', token);
            localStorage.setItem('gh_repo', repo);
            
            document.getElementById('github-config').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('github-branch').textContent = state.github.branch;
            showNotification('Connected', 'success');
            await loadGitHubFiles('');
        } else {
            throw new Error(data.error);
        }
    } catch (error) {
        if (!silent) showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
        state.github.connected = false;
    }
}

function toggleGitHubDropdown() {
    const dropdown = document.getElementById('github-dropdown-menu');
    dropdown.classList.toggle('open');
}

function hideGitHubDropdown() {
    document.getElementById('github-dropdown-menu').classList.remove('open');
}

function disconnectGitHub() {
    state.github.connected = false;
    state.github.token = '';
    state.github.repo = '';
    localStorage.removeItem('gh_token');
    localStorage.removeItem('gh_repo');
    document.getElementById('gh-token').value = '';
    document.getElementById('gh-repo').value = '';
    document.getElementById('github-files').innerHTML = `
        <div class="text-center text-gray-500 mt-8 text-sm p-4">
            <i class="fab fa-github text-4xl mb-2 opacity-50"></i>
            <p>Configure GitHub</p>
            <button id="btn-show-config" class="mt-2 px-4 py-2 bg-gray-800 hover:bg-gray-700 rounded text-xs">Configure</button>
        </div>
    `;
    document.getElementById('btn-show-config').addEventListener('click', showGitHubConfig);
    showNotification('Disconnected from GitHub', 'info');
}

async function showBranchSelector() {
    if (!state.github.connected) {
        showNotification('Not connected to GitHub', 'error');
        return;
    }
    // Fetch branches and show selector
    fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/branches`)
        .then(r => r.json())
        .then(data => {
            if (data.success) {
                const branches = data.branches.map(b => b.name);
                const currentBranch = data.currentBranch;
                const newBranch = prompt(`Current branch: ${currentBranch}\n\nAvailable branches:\n${branches.join('\n')}\n\nEnter branch name to switch:`);
                if (newBranch && branches.includes(newBranch)) {
                    fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/branch`, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                        body: JSON.stringify({ branch: newBranch })
                    })
                    .then(r => r.json())
                    .then(result => {
                        if (result.success) {
                            state.github.branch = newBranch;
                            document.getElementById('github-branch').textContent = newBranch;
                            loadGitHubFiles(state.github.currentPath);
                            showNotification(`Switched to branch: ${newBranch}`, 'success');
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
        });
}

// Export functions globally
window.showGitHubConfig = showGitHubConfig;
window.connectGitHub = connectGitHub;
window.toggleGitHubDropdown = toggleGitHubDropdown;
window.hideGitHubDropdown = hideGitHubDropdown;
window.disconnectGitHub = disconnectGitHub;
window.showBranchSelector = showBranchSelector;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Keyboard Shortcuts Module
// Handles keyboard shortcuts and global key events

function setupKeyboardShortcuts() {
    document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
        if (e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) {
            if (e.key.toLowerCase() === 's') {
                e.preventDefault();
                if (state.editor.visible) saveCurrentFile();
            }
            if (e.key.toLowerCase() === 'f') {
                e.preventDefault();
                toggleSearch('local');
            }
        }
        if (e.key === 'Escape') {
            if (state.dropdown.localOpen) closeDropdownLocal();
            else if (state.dropdown.githubOpen) closeDropdownGithub();
            else if (state.searchActive) toggleSearch();
            else if (state.propertiesOpen) closeProperties();
            else if (document.getElementById('tree-modal').classList.contains('flex')) closeTreeModal();
            else {
                closeEditor();
                hideContextMenu();
                closeInputModal();
                clearSelection();
            }
        }
        // Panel mode switching with keyboard
        if (e.altKey) {
            if (e.key === 's') setPanelMode('storage', 'storage');
            if (e.key === 'g') setPanelMode('github', 'github');
            if (e.key === 'd') setPanelMode('storage', 'github');
            if (e.key === 'x') swapPanels();
        }
    });
}

function setupGlobalTouchHandlers() {
    document.addEventListener('touchmove', function(e) {
        if (e.scale !== 1) e.preventDefault();
    }, { passive: false });
    
    let lastTouchEnd = 0;
    document.addEventListener('touchend', function(e) {
        const now = Date.now();
        if (now - lastTouchEnd <= 300) e.preventDefault();
        lastTouchEnd = now;
    }, false);
}

// Export functions globally
window.setupKeyboardShortcuts = setupKeyboardShortcuts;
window.setupGlobalTouchHandlers = setupGlobalTouchHandlers;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Resizer and Drag-Drop Module
// Handles panel resizing and drag-drop functionality

function setupResizers() {
    const resizer1 = document.getElementById('resizer-1');
    const leftPanel = document.getElementById('left-panel');
    
    let isResizing = false;
    
    function initResize(e) {
        isResizing = true;
        resizer1.classList.add('active');
        e.preventDefault();
    }
    
    resizer1.addEventListener('mousedown', initResize);
    resizer1.addEventListener('touchstart', initResize, { passive: false });
    
    document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
        if (!isResizing) return;
        const width = Math.max(200, Math.min(e.clientX, window.innerWidth * 0.7));
        leftPanel.style.width = width + 'px';
    });
    
    document.addEventListener('touchmove', (e) => {
        if (!isResizing) return;
        const width = Math.max(200, Math.min(e.touches[0].clientX, window.innerWidth * 0.7));
        leftPanel.style.width = width + 'px';
    }, { passive: false });
    
    document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => { isResizing = false; resizer1.classList.remove('active'); });
    document.addEventListener('touchend', () => { isResizing = false; resizer1.classList.remove('active'); });
    
    // Drag and drop
    ['local-files', 'github-files'].forEach(id => {
        const container = document.getElementById(id);
        const targetPanel = id === 'local-files' ? 'local' : 'github';
        
        container.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => { 
            e.preventDefault(); 
            e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'copy'; 
        });
        
        container.addEventListener('drop', async (e) => {
            e.preventDefault();
            const data = e.dataTransfer.getData('application/json');
            if (!data) return;
            const { panel: sourcePanel, file } = JSON.parse(data);
            if (sourcePanel !== targetPanel) await transferFile(sourcePanel, targetPanel, file);
        });
    });
}

function handleDragStart(e, panel, file) {
    e.target.classList.add('dragging');
    e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'copy';
    e.dataTransfer.setData('application/json', JSON.stringify({ panel, file }));
}

function handleDragEnd(e) {
    e.target.classList.remove('dragging');
}

// Export functions globally
window.setupResizers = setupResizers;
window.handleDragStart = handleDragStart;
window.handleDragEnd = handleDragEnd;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/handlers/touch_handlers.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Touch Handlers Module
// Handles touch events, selection, and file interactions

function attachTouchHandlers(item, panel, file, index) {
    let touchStartX = 0;
    let touchStartY = 0;
    let touchStartTime = 0;
    let longPressTimer = null;
    let hasMoved = false;
    const panelState = panel === 'local' ? state.local : state.github;
    
    function startPress(e) {
        const touch = e.touches ? e.touches[0] : e;
        touchStartX = touch.clientX;
        touchStartY = touch.clientY;
        touchStartTime = Date.now();
        hasMoved = false;
        item.classList.add('pressing');
        
        longPressTimer = setTimeout(() => {
            if (!hasMoved) {
                item.classList.remove('pressing');
                if (panelState.selectionMode && panelState.selectedFiles.has(file.name)) {
                    showMultiActionMenu(e, panel);
                } else {
                    showContextMenu(e, panel, file);
                }
            }
        }, LONG_PRESS_DURATION);
    }
    
    function movePress(e) {
        if (!touchStartTime) return;
        const touch = e.touches ? e.touches[0] : e;
        const deltaX = Math.abs(touch.clientX - touchStartX);
        const deltaY = Math.abs(touch.clientY - touchStartY);
        
        if (deltaX > DRAG_THRESHOLD || deltaY > DRAG_THRESHOLD) {
            hasMoved = true;
            item.classList.remove('pressing');
            clearTimeout(longPressTimer);
        }
    }
    
    function endPress(e) {
        const duration = Date.now() - touchStartTime;
        item.classList.remove('pressing');
        clearTimeout(longPressTimer);
        
        if (!hasMoved && duration < LONG_PRESS_DURATION) {
            if (panelState.selectionMode) {
                toggleFileSelection(panel, file.name);
            } else if (file.type === 'directory') {
                openFile(panel, file);
            } else {
                selectFile(panel, index, e);
                setTimeout(() => openFile(panel, file), 50);
            }
        }
        touchStartTime = 0;
    }
    
    item.addEventListener('touchstart', startPress, { passive: true });
    item.addEventListener('touchmove', movePress, { passive: true });
    item.addEventListener('touchend', endPress);
    item.addEventListener('touchcancel', () => {
        item.classList.remove('pressing');
        clearTimeout(longPressTimer);
        touchStartTime = 0;
    });
    
    item.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
        if (e.button === 2) {
            e.preventDefault();
            showContextMenu(e, panel, file);
        }
    });
    
    item.addEventListener('contextmenu', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        showContextMenu(e, panel, file);
    });
    
    item.addEventListener('dragstart', (e) => handleDragStart(e, panel, file));
    item.addEventListener('dragend', handleDragEnd);
    
    item.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.stopPropagation();
        if (panelState.selectionMode) {
            toggleFileSelection(panel, file.name);
        } else {
            selectFile(panel, index, e);
        }
    });
    
    item.addEventListener('dblclick', (e) => {
        e.stopPropagation();
        openFile(panel, file);
    });
}

function selectFile(panel, index, event) {
    const container = document.getElementById(`${panel}-files`);
    const items = container.querySelectorAll('.file-item');
    items.forEach(i => i.classList.remove('selected'));
    items[index].classList.add('selected');
    
    if (panel === 'local') state.local.selected = state.local.files[index];
    else state.github.selected = state.github.files[index];
}

// Export functions globally
window.attachTouchHandlers = attachTouchHandlers;
window.selectFile = selectFile;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/renderers/file_list_renderer.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// File List Renderer Module
// Handles rendering file lists for both local and GitHub panels

function renderFileList(panel, files) {
    const container = document.getElementById(`${panel}-files`);
    container.innerHTML = '';
    
    if (files.length === 0) {
        container.innerHTML = `<div class="text-center text-gray-500 mt-8 text-sm p-4"><i class="fas fa-folder-open text-4xl mb-2 opacity-30"></i><p>Empty</p></div>`;
        return;
    }
    
    const panelState = panel === 'local' ? state.local : state.github;
    
    files.forEach((file, index) => {
        const item = document.createElement('div');
        const isSelected = panelState.selectedFiles.has(file.name);
        const isLastOpened = panelState.lastOpened === file.name;
        
        item.className = `file-item flex items-center gap-3 p-3 rounded-lg cursor-pointer select-none relative overflow-hidden ${isSelected ? 'selected' : ''} ${isLastOpened ? 'last-opened' : ''}`;
        if (!("ontouchstart" in window)) { item.draggable = true; }
        item.dataset.name = file.name;
        item.dataset.type = file.type;
        item.dataset.index = index;
        item.dataset.path = file.path || '';
        
        const icon = getFileIcon(file.name, file.type);
        const size = file.type === 'directory' ? '--' : formatSize(file.size);
        
        item.innerHTML = `
            <div class="file-icon"><i class="${icon} text-xl ${file.type === 'directory' ? 'text-yellow-500' : 'text-blue-400'}"></i></div>
            <div class="file-info">
                <div class="file-name">${file.name}</div>
                <div class="file-meta">${size} • ${formatDate(file.modified)}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="long-press-indicator"></div>
        `;
        
        attachTouchHandlers(item, panel, file, index);
        container.appendChild(item);
    });
}

// Export function globally
window.renderFileList = renderFileList;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/services/file_loader.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// File Loader Module
// Handles loading files from local storage and GitHub

async function loadLocalFiles(path) {
    showLoading('local', true);
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/list?path=${encodeURIComponent(path)}`);
        const data = await response.json();
        if (!data.success) throw new Error(data.error);
        state.local.files = data.files;
        state.local.currentPath = path;
        renderFileList('local', data.files);
        updateBreadcrumbElement(document.getElementById('local-breadcrumb'), 'local', path);
        document.getElementById('local-count').textContent = `${data.files.length} items`;
        document.getElementById('local-path').textContent = path;
    } catch (error) {
        showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    } finally {
        showLoading('local', false);
    }
}

async function loadGitHubFiles(path = '') {
    if (!state.github.connected) return;
    showLoading('github', true);
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/list?path=${encodeURIComponent(path)}`);
        const data = await response.json();
        if (!data.success) throw new Error(data.error);
        state.github.files = data.files;
        state.github.currentPath = path;
        renderFileList('github', data.files);
        updateBreadcrumbElement(document.getElementById('github-breadcrumb'), 'github', path);
        document.getElementById('github-count').textContent = `${data.files.length} items`;
    } catch (error) {
        showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    } finally {
        showLoading('github', false);
    }
}

function showLoading(panel, show) {
    document.getElementById(`${panel}-files`).style.opacity = show ? '0.5' : '1';
}

function refreshPanel(panel) {
    if (panel === 'local' || (panel === 'left' && state.panelMode.left === 'storage')) {
        loadLocalFiles(state.local.currentPath);
    } else {
        loadGitHubFiles(state.github.currentPath);
    }
}

// Export functions globally
window.loadLocalFiles = loadLocalFiles;
window.loadGitHubFiles = loadGitHubFiles;
window.showLoading = showLoading;
window.refreshPanel = refreshPanel;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/services/server_health.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Server Health Check Module
// Handles server connectivity monitoring and status updates

async function checkServerHealth() {
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/health`);
        const data = await response.json();
        updateServerStatus(data.status === 'ok' ? 'connected' : 'error', data.status === 'ok' ? 'Connected' : 'Error');
    } catch (err) {
        updateServerStatus('error', 'Offline');
        showNotification('Server offline', 'error', 3000);
    }
}

function updateServerStatus(status, text) {
    const indicator = document.getElementById('server-status');
    const statusText = document.getElementById('status-text');
    const colors = { connected: 'bg-green-500', error: 'bg-red-500', connecting: 'bg-yellow-500' };
    indicator.className = `w-2 h-2 rounded-full ${colors[status] || 'bg-gray-500'} status-pulse`;
    statusText.textContent = text;
}

// Export functions globally
window.checkServerHealth = checkServerHealth;
window.updateServerStatus = updateServerStatus;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Global State Management Module

const API_BASE = window.location.origin + '/api';
const LONG_PRESS_DURATION = 500;

// Panel modes: 'storage' | 'github'
const state = {
    panelMode: {
        left: 'storage',
        right: 'github'
    },
    local: {
        currentPath: '/storage/emulated/0',
        files: [],
        selected: null,
        selectionMode: false,
        selectedFiles: new Set(),
        clipboard: null,
        clipboardAction: null,
        lastOpened: null
    },

        token: localStorage.getItem('gh_token') || '',
        repo: localStorage.getItem('gh_repo') || '',
        currentPath: '',
        files: [],
        selected: null,
        selectionMode: false,
        selectedFiles: new Set(),
        clipboard: null,
        clipboardAction: null,

    },

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/transfer/transfer_operations.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Transfer Operations Module
// Handles file transfer between local storage and GitHub

async function transferFile(from, to, file) {
    if (file.type === 'directory') {
        showNotification('Folder transfer not supported yet', 'warning');
        return;
    }
    
    showTransferProgress(true, `Transferring ${file.name}...`);
    
    try {
        if (from === 'local' && to === 'github') {
            await fetch(`${API_BASE}/transfer/local-to-github`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    localPath: `${state.local.currentPath}/${file.name}`,
                    githubPath: `${state.github.currentPath ? state.github.currentPath + '/' : ''}${file.name}`
                })
            });
        } else if (from === 'github' && to === 'local') {
            await fetch(`${API_BASE}/transfer/github-to-local`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    githubPath: file.path || file.name,
                    localPath: `${state.local.currentPath}/${file.name}`
                })
            });
        }
        
        showTransferProgress(false);
        showNotification('Transferred', 'success');
        refreshPanel(to);
    } catch (error) {
        showTransferProgress(false);
        showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    }
}

function showTransferProgress(show, text) {
    const modal = document.getElementById('transfer-modal');
    const progress = document.getElementById('transfer-progress');
    
    if (show) {
        modal.classList.remove('hidden');
        modal.classList.add('flex');
        document.getElementById('transfer-text').textContent = text;
        progress.style.width = '30%';
        setTimeout(() => progress.style.width = '70%', 200);
    } else {
        progress.style.width = '100%';
        setTimeout(() => {
            modal.classList.add('hidden');
            modal.classList.remove('flex');
            progress.style.width = '0%';
        }, 300);
    }
}

async function openFile(panel, file) {
    if (file.type === 'directory') {
        let newPath;
        if (panel === 'local') {
            const current = state.local.currentPath;
            newPath = current.endsWith('/') ? `${current}${file.name}` : `${current}/${file.name}`;
        } else {
            const current = state.github.currentPath;
            newPath = current ? `${current}/${file.name}` : file.name;
        }
        navigateTo(panel, newPath);
        return;
    }
    
    // Mark as last opened
    if (panel === 'local') {
        state.local.lastOpened = file.name;
    } else {
        state.github.lastOpened = file.name;
    }
    
    const textExts = ['txt', 'md', 'js', 'html', 'css', 'json', 'py', 'java', 'c', 'cpp', 'go', 'rs', 'ts', 'xml', 'yaml', 'yml'];
    const ext = file.name.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
    
    if (!textExts.includes(ext)) {
        showNotification('Binary file - cannot edit', 'warning');
        return;
    }
    
    openEditor(panel, file);
}

async function deleteFile(panel, file) {
    if (!confirm(`Delete "${file.name}"?`)) return;
    
    try {
        if (panel === 'local') {
            await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/delete`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ path: `${state.local.currentPath}/${file.name}` })
            });
        } else {
            const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/delete`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ 
                    path: file.path || file.name, 
                    sha: file.sha, 
                    message: `Delete ${file.name}` 
                })
            });
            
            if (!response.ok) {
                const error = await response.json();
                throw new Error(error.error || 'Delete failed');
            }
        }
        
        showNotification('Deleted', 'success');
        refreshPanel(panel);
    } catch (error) {
        showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
    }
}

async function handlePaste(panel) {
    const clipboard = panel === 'local' ? state.local.clipboard : state.github.clipboard;
    if (!clipboard) { 
        showNotification('Clipboard empty', 'warning'); 
        return; 
    }
    
    if (panel === 'local' && state.local.clipboardAction === 'copy') {
        try {
            const content = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/read?path=${encodeURIComponent(state.local.currentPath + '/' + clipboard.name)}`).then(r => r.text());
            await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/write`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ path: state.local.currentPath + '/' + clipboard.name + '_copy', content })
            });
            refreshPanel('local');
            showNotification('Pasted', 'success');
        } catch (error) {
            showNotification(`Error: ${error.message}`, 'error');
        }
    }
}

// Export functions globally
window.transferFile = transferFile;
window.showTransferProgress = showTransferProgress;
window.openFile = openFile;
window.deleteFile = deleteFile;
window.handlePaste = handlePaste;
