━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/ui/breadcrumb_manager.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Breadcrumb Manager Module
// Handles breadcrumb navigation for local and GitHub panels

function updateBreadcrumbElement(container, panel, path, isDropdown = false) {
    container.innerHTML = '';
    
    if (panel === 'local' || panel === 'drop-local') {
        const basePath = '/storage/emulated/0';
        const parts = path.replace(basePath, '').split('/').filter(p => p);
        let currentPath = basePath;
        
        const root = document.createElement('span');
        root.className = 'breadcrumb-item';
        root.textContent = '/';
        root.onclick = () => {
            state.local.currentPath = basePath;
            loadLocalFiles(basePath).then(() => {
                if (isDropdown) renderDropdownFiles('local');
            });
        };
        container.appendChild(root);
        
        parts.forEach(part => {
            const sep = document.createElement('span');
            sep.className = 'text-gray-600 px-1';
            sep.textContent = '/';
            container.appendChild(sep);
            
            currentPath += '/' + part;
            const span = document.createElement('span');
            span.className = 'breadcrumb-item';
            span.textContent = part;
            const snap = currentPath;
            span.onclick = () => {
                state.local.currentPath = snap;
                loadLocalFiles(snap).then(() => {
                    if (isDropdown) renderDropdownFiles('local');
                });
            };
            container.appendChild(span);
        });
    } else {
        const parts = path ? path.split('/').filter(p => p) : [];
        
        const root = document.createElement('span');
        root.className = 'breadcrumb-item text-green-400';
        root.textContent = 'root';
        root.onclick = () => {
            state.github.currentPath = '';
            loadGitHubFiles('').then(() => {
                if (isDropdown) renderDropdownFiles('github');
            });
        };
        container.appendChild(root);
        
        let currentPath = '';
        parts.forEach(part => {
            const sep = document.createElement('span');
            sep.className = 'text-gray-600 px-1';
            sep.textContent = '/';
            container.appendChild(sep);
            
            currentPath = currentPath ? `${currentPath}/${part}` : part;
            const span = document.createElement('span');
            span.className = 'breadcrumb-item text-green-400';
            span.textContent = part;
            const snap = currentPath;
            span.onclick = () => {
                state.github.currentPath = snap;
                loadGitHubFiles(snap).then(() => {
                    if (isDropdown) renderDropdownFiles('github');
                });
            };
            container.appendChild(span);
        });
    }
}

function navigateTo(panel, path) {
    if (panel === 'local' || (panel === 'left' && state.panelMode.left === 'storage') || (panel === 'right' && state.panelMode.right === 'storage')) {
        loadLocalFiles(path);
    } else {
        loadGitHubFiles(path);
    }
}

function navigateUp(panel) {
    if (panel === 'local' || (panel === 'left' && state.panelMode.left === 'storage')) {
        const current = state.local.currentPath;
        if (current === '/storage/emulated/0' || current === '/') return;
        const parent = current.substring(0, current.lastIndexOf('/')) || '/storage/emulated/0';
        loadLocalFiles(parent);
    } else if (panel === 'github' || (panel === 'right' && state.panelMode.right === 'github')) {
        const current = state.github.currentPath;
        if (!current) return;
        const lastSlash = current.lastIndexOf('/');
        const parent = lastSlash > 0 ? current.substring(0, lastSlash) : '';
        loadGitHubFiles(parent);
    }
}

// Export functions globally
window.updateBreadcrumbElement = updateBreadcrumbElement;
window.navigateTo = navigateTo;
window.navigateUp = navigateUp;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/ui/context_menu.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Context Menu Module
// Handles context menu display and actions

function showContextMenu(e, panel, file) {
    state.contextMenuTarget = { panel, file };
    
    const menu = document.getElementById('context-menu');
    const overlay = document.getElementById('menu-overlay');
    const header = document.getElementById('ctx-header');
    
    // Reset menu items visibility
    document.getElementById('ctx-open').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('ctx-edit').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('ctx-copy').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('ctx-cut').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('ctx-paste').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('ctx-rename').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('ctx-delete').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('ctx-transfer').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('ctx-properties').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('ctx-tree').style.display = file.type === 'directory' ? 'flex' : 'none';
    
    header.textContent = file.name;
    
    const x = Math.min(e.clientX || e.touches?.[0]?.clientX || 100, window.innerWidth - 220);
    const y = Math.min(e.clientY || e.touches?.[0]?.clientY || 100, window.innerHeight - 450);
    
    menu.style.left = x + 'px';
    menu.style.top = y + 'px';
    menu.classList.remove('hidden');
    overlay.classList.add('active');
}

function hideContextMenu() {
    document.getElementById('context-menu').classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('menu-overlay').classList.remove('active');
}

function showMultiActionMenu(e, panel) {
    const menu = document.getElementById('context-menu');
    const header = document.getElementById('ctx-header');
    const panelState = panel === 'local' ? state.local : state.github;
    
    header.textContent = `${panelState.selectedFiles.size} items selected`;
    
    // Hide single-item actions
    document.getElementById('ctx-open').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('ctx-edit').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('ctx-copy').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('ctx-cut').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('ctx-paste').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('ctx-rename').style.display = 'none';
    
    // Show batch actions
    document.getElementById('ctx-delete').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('ctx-transfer').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('ctx-properties').style.display = 'flex';
    
    const x = Math.min(e.clientX || e.touches?.[0]?.clientX || 100, window.innerWidth - 220);
    const y = Math.min(e.clientY || e.touches?.[0]?.clientY || 100, window.innerHeight - 350);
    
    menu.style.left = x + 'px';
    menu.style.top = y + 'px';
    menu.classList.remove('hidden');
    document.getElementById('menu-overlay').classList.add('active');
    
    state.contextMenuTarget = { panel, multiSelect: true };
}

async function ctxAction(action) {
    const { panel, file, multiSelect } = state.contextMenuTarget;
    hideContextMenu();
    
    if (multiSelect) {
        switch(action) {
            case 'delete':
                await batchDelete();
                break;
            case 'transfer':
                await batchTransfer();
                break;
            case 'properties':
                batchProperties();
                break;
        }
        return;
    }
    
    switch(action) {
        case 'open':
        case 'edit':
            await openFile(panel, file);
            break;
        case 'copy':
            if (panel === 'local') { 
                state.local.clipboard = file; 
                state.local.clipboardAction = 'copy'; 
            } else { 
                state.github.clipboard = file; 
                state.github.clipboardAction = 'copy'; 
            }
            showNotification('Copied', 'info');
            break;
        case 'cut':
            if (panel === 'local') { 
                state.local.clipboard = file; 
                state.local.clipboardAction = 'cut'; 
            } else { 
                state.github.clipboard = file; 
                state.github.clipboardAction = 'cut'; 
            }
            showNotification('Cut', 'info');
            break;
        case 'paste':
            await handlePaste(panel);
            break;
        case 'rename':
            renameInline(panel, file);
            break;
        case 'delete':
            await deleteFile(panel, file);
            break;
        case 'transfer':
            await transferFile(panel, panel === 'local' ? 'github' : 'local', file);
            break;
        case 'properties':
            showProperties(panel, file);
            break;
        case 'tree':
            showTreeView(panel, file);
            break;
    }
}

// Export functions globally
window.showContextMenu = showContextMenu;
window.hideContextMenu = hideContextMenu;
window.showMultiActionMenu = showMultiActionMenu;
window.ctxAction = ctxAction;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/ui/dropdown_manager.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Dropdown Manager Module
// Handles dropdown panel functionality for local and GitHub

function toggleDropdownLocal() {
    const drop = document.getElementById('dropdown-local');
    const btn = document.getElementById('btn-dropdown-local');
    
    if (state.dropdown.localOpen) {
        closeDropdownLocal();
    } else {
        closeDropdownGithub();
        drop.classList.add('open');
        btn.classList.add('active');
        state.dropdown.localOpen = true;
        renderDropdownFiles('local');
    }
}

function closeDropdownLocal() {
    document.getElementById('dropdown-local').classList.remove('open');
    document.getElementById('btn-dropdown-local').classList.remove('active');
    state.dropdown.localOpen = false;
}

function toggleDropdownGithub() {
    const drop = document.getElementById('dropdown-github');
    const btn = document.getElementById('btn-dropdown-github');
    
    if (state.dropdown.githubOpen) {
        closeDropdownGithub();
    } else {
        closeDropdownLocal();
        drop.classList.add('open');
        btn.classList.add('active');
        state.dropdown.githubOpen = true;
        renderDropdownFiles('github');
    }
}

function closeDropdownGithub() {
    document.getElementById('dropdown-github').classList.remove('open');
    document.getElementById('btn-dropdown-github').classList.remove('active');
    state.dropdown.githubOpen = false;
}

function renderDropdownFiles(panel) {
    const isLocal = panel === 'local';
    const files = isLocal ? state.local.files : state.github.files;
    const container = document.getElementById(`drop-${panel}-files`);
    const breadcrumb = document.getElementById(`drop-${panel}-breadcrumb`);
    
    updateBreadcrumbElement(breadcrumb, panel, isLocal ? state.local.currentPath : state.github.currentPath, true);
    
    container.innerHTML = '';
    
    if (files.length === 0) {
        container.innerHTML = `<div class="text-center text-gray-500 mt-8 text-sm p-4"><i class="fas fa-folder-open text-4xl mb-2 opacity-30"></i><p>Empty</p></div>`;
        return;
    }
    
    files.forEach((file, index) => {
        const item = document.createElement('div');
        item.className = 'file-item flex items-center gap-3 p-3 rounded-lg cursor-pointer select-none relative overflow-hidden';
        item.dataset.name = file.name;
        item.dataset.type = file.type;
        
        const icon = getFileIcon(file.name, file.type);
        const size = file.type === 'directory' ? '--' : formatSize(file.size);
        
        item.innerHTML = `
            <div class="file-icon"><i class="${icon} text-xl ${file.type === 'directory' ? 'text-yellow-500' : 'text-blue-400'}"></i></div>
            <div class="file-info">
                <div class="file-name">${file.name}</div>
                <div class="file-meta">${size} • ${formatDate(file.modified)}</div>
            </div>
        `;
        
        attachDropdownTouchHandlers(item, panel, file);
        container.appendChild(item);
    });
}

function attachDropdownTouchHandlers(item, panel, file) {
    item.addEventListener('click', () => {
        if (file.type === 'directory') {
            const targetPanel = panel === 'drop-local' ? 'local' : 'github';
            const current = targetPanel === 'local' ? state.local.currentPath : state.github.currentPath;
            const newPath = current ? `${current}/${file.name}` : file.name;
            
            if (targetPanel === 'local') {
                state.local.currentPath = newPath;
                loadLocalFiles(newPath).then(() => renderDropdownFiles('local'));
            } else {
                state.github.currentPath = newPath;
                loadGitHubFiles(newPath).then(() => renderDropdownFiles('github'));
            }
        }
    });
}

// Export functions globally
window.toggleDropdownLocal = toggleDropdownLocal;
window.closeDropdownLocal = closeDropdownLocal;
window.toggleDropdownGithub = toggleDropdownGithub;
window.closeDropdownGithub = closeDropdownGithub;
window.renderDropdownFiles = renderDropdownFiles;
window.attachDropdownTouchHandlers = attachDropdownTouchHandlers;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/ui/notification_system.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Notification System Module
// Handles displaying notifications to the user

function showNotification(message, type = 'info', duration = 3000) {
    const container = document.getElementById('notifications');
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    
    const colors = { success: 'bg-green-600', error: 'bg-red-600', warning: 'bg-yellow-600', info: 'bg-blue-600' };
    const icons = { success: 'fa-check-circle', error: 'fa-exclamation-circle', warning: 'fa-exclamation-triangle', info: 'fa-info-circle' };
    
    div.className = `notification ${colors[type]} text-white px-4 py-3 rounded-lg shadow-lg flex items-center gap-3 pointer-events-auto`;
    div.innerHTML = `<i class="fas ${icons[type]}"></i><span class="flex-1">${message}</span>`;
    
    container.appendChild(div);
    setTimeout(() => {
        div.style.opacity = '0';
        div.style.transform = 'translateX(100%)';
        setTimeout(() => div.remove(), 300);
    }, duration);
}

// Export function globally
window.showNotification = showNotification;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/client/index/modules/ui/properties_panel.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Properties Panel Module
// Handles displaying file/folder properties

async function showProperties(panel, file, isMulti = false) {
    const panelState = panel === 'local' ? state.local : state.github;
    const propertiesPanel = document.getElementById('properties-panel');
    const propertiesContent = document.getElementById('properties-content');
    const propertiesTitle = document.getElementById('properties-title');
    
    if (isMulti) {
        propertiesTitle.textContent = 'Multiple Items';
        const panelState = panel === 'local' ? state.local : state.github;
        const files = Array.from(panelState.selectedFiles).map(name => {
            return panelState.files.find(f => f.name === name);
        }).filter(Boolean);
        
        const totalSize = files.reduce((sum, f) => sum + (f.size || 0), 0);
        const fileCount = files.filter(f => f.type === 'file').length;
        const folderCount = files.filter(f => f.type === 'directory').length;
        
        propertiesContent.innerHTML = `
            <div class="property-row">
                <span class="property-label">Items</span>
                <span class="property-value">${files.length}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="property-row">
                <span class="property-label">Files</span>
                <span class="property-value">${fileCount}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="property-row">
                <span class="property-label">Folders</span>
                <span class="property-value">${folderCount}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="property-row">
                <span class="property-label">Total Size</span>
                <span class="property-value">${formatSize(totalSize)}</span>
            </div>
        `;
    } else if (panel === 'local') {
        propertiesTitle.textContent = file.name;
        
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/local/stats?path=${encodeURIComponent(state.local.currentPath + '/' + file.name)}`);
            const data = await response.json();
            const stats = data.stats;
            
            propertiesContent.innerHTML = `
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Name</span>
                    <span class="property-value copyable" data-value="${file.name}">${file.name}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Path</span>
                    <span class="property-value copyable path-copy" data-value="${state.local.currentPath}/${file.name}">${state.local.currentPath}/${file.name}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Type</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${file.type}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Size</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${formatSize(stats.size)}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Modified</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${formatDate(stats.modified)}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Created</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${formatDate(stats.created)}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Permissions</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${stats.permissions}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Owner</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${stats.owner}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Group</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${stats.group}</span>
                </div>
                ${file.type === 'directory' ? `
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Contents</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${stats.fileCount} files, ${stats.folderCount} folders</span>
                </div>
                ` : ''}
            `;
        } catch (err) {
            propertiesContent.innerHTML = `<div class="p-4 text-red-400">Error loading properties</div>`;
        }
    } else {
        propertiesTitle.textContent = file.name;
        
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/github/stats?path=${encodeURIComponent(file.path || file.name)}`);
            const data = await response.json();
            const stats = data.stats;
            
            propertiesContent.innerHTML = `
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Name</span>
                    <span class="property-value copyable" data-value="${stats.name}">${stats.name}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Path</span>
                    <span class="property-value copyable path-copy" data-value="${stats.path}">${stats.path}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Size</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${formatSize(stats.size)}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">SHA</span>
                    <span class="property-value copyable" data-value="${stats.sha}">${stats.sha.substring(0, 16)}...</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Branch</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${stats.branch}</span>
                </div>
                ${stats.commitDate ? `
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Last Commit</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${formatDate(stats.commitDate)}</span>
                </div>
                ` : ''}
                ${stats.author ? `
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Author</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${stats.author}</span>
                </div>
                ` : ''}
                ${stats.download_url ? `
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Download</span>
                    <span class="property-value copyable" data-value="${stats.download_url}">Copy URL</span>
                </div>
                ` : ''}
            `;
        } catch (err) {
            propertiesContent.innerHTML = `
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Name</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${file.name}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Path</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${file.path || file.name}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">Size</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${formatSize(file.size)}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="property-row">
                    <span class="property-label">SHA</span>
                    <span class="property-value">${file.sha ? file.sha.substring(0, 16) + '...' : 'N/A'}</span>
                </div>
            `;
        }
    }
    
    // Add click handlers for copy
    propertiesContent.querySelectorAll('.copyable').forEach(el => {
        el.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const value = el.dataset.value || el.textContent;
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(value).then(() => {
                el.classList.add('copied');
                el.textContent = 'Copied!';
                setTimeout(() => {
                    el.classList.remove('copied');
                    el.textContent = value.length > 30 ? value.substring(0, 30) + '...' : value;
                }, 1500);
            });
        });
    });
    
    // Long press for path copy
    propertiesContent.querySelectorAll('.path-copy').forEach(el => {
        let longPressTimer;
        el.addEventListener('touchstart', () => {
            longPressTimer = setTimeout(() => {
                const fullPath = el.dataset.value;
                navigator.clipboard.writeText(fullPath).then(() => {
                    showNotification('Full path copied', 'success');
                });
            }, 500);
        });
        el.addEventListener('touchend', () => clearTimeout(longPressTimer));
    });
    
    propertiesPanel.classList.add('open');
    state.propertiesOpen = true;
}

function closeProperties() {
    document.getElementById('properties-panel').classList.remove('open');
    state.propertiesOpen = false;
}

// Export functions globally
window.showProperties = showProperties;
window.closeProperties = closeProperties;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// File Utility Functions Module
// Provides helper functions for file operations and formatting

function getFileIcon(name, type) {
    if (type === 'directory') return 'fas fa-folder';
    const ext = name.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
    const icons = {
        'js': 'fab fa-js text-yellow-400',
        'html': 'fab fa-html5 text-orange-500',
        'css': 'fab fa-css3 text-blue-500',
        'json': 'fas fa-code text-gray-400',
        'md': 'fas fa-markdown text-white',
        'txt': 'fas fa-file-alt text-gray-400',
        'py': 'fab fa-python text-blue-300',
        'java': 'fab fa-java text-red-400',
        'png': 'fas fa-image text-purple-400',
        'jpg': 'fas fa-image text-purple-400',
        'jpeg': 'fas fa-image text-purple-400',
        'gif': 'fas fa-image text-purple-400',
        'pdf': 'fas fa-file-pdf text-red-500',
        'zip': 'fas fa-file-archive text-yellow-600'
    };
    return icons[ext] || 'fas fa-file text-gray-400';
}

function formatSize(bytes) {
    if (!bytes || bytes === 0) return '0 B';
    const k = 1024;
    const sizes = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
    const i = Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k));
    return parseFloat((bytes / Math.pow(k, i)).toFixed(1)) + ' ' + sizes[i];
}

function formatDate(dateStr) {
    if (!dateStr) return 'Unknown';
    const date = new Date(dateStr);
    const now = new Date();
    const diff = now - date;
    
    // If today, show time
    if (diff < 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 && date.getDate() === now.getDate()) {
        return date.toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
    }
    
    // If this year, show month and day
    if (date.getFullYear() === now.getFullYear()) {
        return date.toLocaleDateString([], { month: 'short', day: 'numeric' });
    }
    
    return date.toLocaleDateString();
}

function getLanguage(filename) {
    const ext = filename.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
    const langs = { 
        js: 'javascript', 
        ts: 'typescript', 
        html: 'html', 
        css: 'css', 
        json: 'json', 
        md: 'markdown', 
        py: 'python', 
        java: 'java', 
        cpp: 'cpp', 
        c: 'c', 
        go: 'go', 
        rs: 'rust', 
        xml: 'xml', 
        yaml: 'yaml', 
        yml: 'yaml' 
    };
    return langs[ext] || 'plaintext';
}

// Export functions globally
window.getFileIcon = getFileIcon;
window.formatSize = formatSize;
window.formatDate = formatDate;
window.getLanguage = getLanguage;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
# MT-Git Manager v2.0

A powerful dual-panel file manager with GitHub integration, designed for professional file management across local storage and GitHub repositories.

## Features

### Core Functionality
- **Dual-Panel Interface**: Side-by-side file management with independent navigation
- **Panel Mode Switching**: Switch between Storage/Storage, GitHub/GitHub, or Storage/GitHub modes
- **Panel Swap**: Instantly swap panel contents with one click
- **Multi-Select System**: Long-press to enter selection mode, tap to add/remove from selection
- **Batch Operations**: Transfer, delete, or view properties for multiple files at once

### File Operations
- **Inline Folder Creation**: Create folders directly in the file list without modals
- **Inline Rename**: Rename files with inline editing interface
- **Drag & Drop**: Transfer files between panels via drag and drop
- **Copy/Paste**: Clipboard operations for local files

### GitHub Integration
- **Full Repository Management**: Browse, edit, create, delete files in GitHub repos
- **Rename with Backup**: GitHub renames create automatic local backups for safety
- **Branch Switching**: Switch between branches from the dropdown menu
- **Commit History**: View last commit info in file properties

### Advanced Features
- **Smart Search**: Filter by name patterns (*.js), or use advanced queries
- **File Properties**: Detailed properties panel with one-tap copy functionality
- **Directory Tree View**: Visual tree representation of directory structure
- **Last Opened Indicator**: Visual highlight for recently accessed files
- **Monaco Editor**: Full-featured code editor with syntax highlighting

### Keyboard Shortcuts
- `Ctrl+S`: Save current file
- `Ctrl+F`: Open search
- `Alt+S`: Set Storage | Storage mode
- `Alt+G`: Set GitHub | GitHub mode
- `Alt+D`: Set Storage | GitHub mode (default)
- `Alt+X`: Swap panels
- `Escape`: Close editor/modals/clear selection

## Installation

```bash
# Navigate to server directory
cd server

# Install dependencies
npm install

# Start server
npm start

# Or for development with auto-restart
npm run dev
```

The server will start on `http://localhost:8080`.

## Configuration

### Server Config (`server/config/config.json`)
```json
{
  "server": {
    "port": 8080,
    "host": "0.0.0.0"
  },
  "security": {
    "basePath": "/storage/emulated/0",
    "maxFileSize": 104857600
  },
  "github": {
    "defaultBranch": "main",
    "timeout": 30000
  }
}
```

### GitHub Setup
1. Generate a GitHub Personal Access Token with `repo` scope
2. Enter token and repository (format: `owner/repo`) in the GitHub panel
3. Click Connect

## API Endpoints

### Local Filesystem
- `GET /api/local/list?path=` - List directory contents
- `GET /api/local/read?path=` - Read file content
- `GET /api/local/stats?path=` - Get file statistics
- `GET /api/local/tree?path=` - Get directory tree
- `POST /api/local/write` - Write file
- `POST /api/local/delete` - Delete file/folder
- `POST /api/local/rename` - Rename file
- `POST /api/local/mkdir` - Create directory

### GitHub
- `POST /api/github/connect` - Connect to GitHub
- `GET /api/github/list?path=` - List repository contents
- `GET /api/github/read?path=` - Read file content
- `GET /api/github/stats?path=` - Get file stats with commit info
- `POST /api/github/create` - Create file
- `POST /api/github/update` - Update file
- `POST /api/github/delete` - Delete file
- `POST /api/github/rename` - Rename file (with backup)
- `GET /api/github/branches` - List branches
- `POST /api/github/branch` - Switch branch

### Transfer
- `POST /api/transfer/local-to-github` - Transfer file to GitHub
- `POST /api/transfer/github-to-local` - Transfer file from GitHub
- `POST /api/transfer/batch` - Batch transfer multiple files

## Safety Features

### GitHub Rename Backup
Every GitHub rename operation automatically creates a backup:
- Location: `system/github_panel/renamed/`
- Contains: Original file, new file, metadata.json
- Metadata includes: old/new names, paths, timestamp, SHA, branch

### Error Protection
- All operations validate before execution
- Delete operations require confirmation
- Transfer progress is displayed
- Failed operations show detailed error messages

## Mobile Optimized

- Touch-friendly interface with proper touch targets (44px minimum)
- Long-press for context menus
- Swipe gestures for navigation
- Responsive design adapts to screen size
- Prevents zoom/scroll conflicts

## Browser Compatibility

- Chrome/Edge 90+
- Firefox 88+
- Safari 14+
- Mobile browsers (iOS Safari, Chrome Android)

## License

MIT License - See LICENSE file for details

## Changelog

### v2.0.0
- Complete rewrite with dual-panel architecture
- Added multi-select and batch operations
- Added inline rename and folder creation
- Added GitHub rename with backup system
- Added file properties panel
- Added directory tree view
- Added smart search functionality
- Added panel mode switching and swap
- Added GitHub settings dropdown
- Improved mobile touch support
- Added Monaco Editor integration

// server/routes/github.js - GitHub API routes
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const githubService = require('../services/githubService');

// POST /api/github/connect
router.post('/connect', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { token, repo } = req.body;
        
        if (!token || !repo) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Token and repo (owner/name) required'
            });
        }

        const repoInfo = await githubService.validateConnection(token, repo);
        githubService.setCredentials(token, repo);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'Connected to GitHub successfully',
            repo: repoInfo,
            branch: githubService.branch
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(401).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// GET /api/github/list?path=
router.get('/list', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path = '' } = req.query;
        
        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub. Call /connect first.'
            });
        }

        const files = await githubService.listContents(path);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            path: path,
            files: files
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// GET /api/github/read?path=
router.get('/read', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path } = req.query;
        
        if (!path) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path parameter required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub'
            });
        }

        const content = await githubService.getFileContent(path);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            path: path,
            content: content,
            encoding: 'utf-8'
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// GET /api/github/stats?path=
router.get('/stats', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path } = req.query;
        
        if (!path) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path parameter required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub'
            });
        }

        const fileInfo = await githubService.getFileInfo(path);
        const commitInfo = await githubService.getFileCommitInfo(path);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            path: path,
            stats: {
                name: fileInfo.name,
                path: fileInfo.path,
                size: fileInfo.size || 0,
                sha: fileInfo.sha,
                download_url: fileInfo.download_url,
                html_url: fileInfo.html_url,
                commitDate: commitInfo?.date,
                author: commitInfo?.author,
                branch: githubService.branch
            }
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// POST /api/github/create
router.post('/create', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path: filePath, content, message = `Create ${filePath} via MT-Git Manager` } = req.body;
        
        if (!filePath || content === undefined) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path and content required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub'
            });
        }

        const result = await githubService.createFile(filePath, content, message);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'File created successfully',
            commit: result.commit,
            content: result.content
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// POST /api/github/update
router.post('/update', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path: filePath, content, sha, message = `Update ${filePath} via MT-Git Manager` } = req.body;
        
        if (!filePath || content === undefined || !sha) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path, content, and sha required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub'
            });
        }

        const result = await githubService.updateFile(filePath, content, sha, message);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'File updated successfully',
            commit: result.commit,
            content: result.content
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

            success: true,
            message: 'File deleted successfully',
            commit: result.commit
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

router.post('/rename', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { oldPath, newPath, sha, message } = req.body;
        
        if (!oldPath || !newPath || !sha) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'oldPath, newPath, and sha required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub'
            });
        }

        const result = await githubService.renameFile(oldPath, newPath, sha, message);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'File renamed successfully',
            ...result
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

router.get('/branches', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub'
            });
        }

        const branches = await githubService.listBranches();
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            branches: branches,
            currentBranch: githubService.branch
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }

// POST /api/github/branch
router.post('/branch', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { branch } = req.body;
        
        if (!branch) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Branch name required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub'
            });
        }

        githubService.setBranch(branch);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: `Switched to branch: ${branch}`,
            branch: branch
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

module.exports = router;

// server/routes/localStorage.js - Local filesystem routes
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const filesystemService = require('../services/filesystemService');

// GET /api/local/list?path=/storage/emulated/0/Documents
router.get('/list', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path: dirPath } = req.query;
        
        if (!dirPath) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path parameter required'
            });
        }

        const files = await filesystemService.listDirectory(dirPath);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            path: dirPath,
            files: files
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// GET /api/local/tree?path=/storage/emulated/0
router.get('/tree', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path: dirPath, maxDepth = 10 } = req.query;
        
        if (!dirPath) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path parameter required'
            });
        }

        const tree = await filesystemService.getDirectoryTree(dirPath, 0, parseInt(maxDepth));
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            path: dirPath,
            tree: tree
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// GET /api/local/stats?path=/storage/emulated/0/file.txt
router.get('/stats', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path: filePath } = req.query;
        
        if (!filePath) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path parameter required'
            });
        }

        const stats = await filesystemService.getFileStats(filePath);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            path: filePath,
            stats: stats
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// GET /api/local/read?path=/storage/emulated/0/file.txt
router.get('/read', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path: filePath } = req.query;
        
        if (!filePath) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path parameter required'
            });
        }

        const content = await filesystemService.readFile(filePath);
        
        const ext = filePath.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
        const mimeTypes = {
            'txt': 'text/plain',
            'json': 'application/json',
            'js': 'application/javascript',
            'html': 'text/html',
            'css': 'text/css',
            'md': 'text/markdown'
        };
        
        res.setHeader('Content-Type', mimeTypes[ext] || 'text/plain');
        res.send(content);
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// POST /api/local/write
router.post('/write', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path: filePath, content } = req.body;
        
        if (!filePath || content === undefined) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path and content required'
            });
        }

        await filesystemService.writeFile(filePath, content);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'File written successfully',
            path: filePath
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// GET /api/local/download?path=...
router.get('/download', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path: filePath } = req.query;
        
        if (!filePath) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path parameter required'
            });
        }

        const fileName = filePath.split('/').pop();
        const content = await filesystemService.readFile(filePath);
        
        res.setHeader('Content-Disposition', `attachment; filename="${fileName}"`);
        res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'application/octet-stream');
        res.send(content);
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

            success: true,
            roots: roots
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/server/routes/transfer.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// server/routes/transfer.js - File transfer routes
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const filesystemService = require('../services/filesystemService');
const githubService = require('../services/githubService');

// POST /api/transfer/local-to-github
router.post('/local-to-github', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { localPath, githubPath, message } = req.body;
        
        if (!localPath || !githubPath) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Both localPath and githubPath required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'GitHub not connected'
            });
        }

        console.log(`[Transfer] Reading local file: ${localPath}`);
        const content = await filesystemService.readFile(localPath);
        
        let sha = null;
        try {
            const existingFile = await githubService.getFileInfo(githubPath);
            sha = existingFile.sha;
        } catch (err) {
            // File doesn't exist, will create new
        }

        console.log(`[Transfer] Writing to GitHub: ${githubPath}`);
        let result;
        const commitMessage = message || `Transfer ${localPath.split('/').pop()} via MT-Git Manager`;
        
        if (sha) {
            result = await githubService.updateFile(githubPath, content, sha, commitMessage);
        } else {
            result = await githubService.createFile(githubPath, content, commitMessage);
        }

        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'Transfer completed successfully',
            source: localPath,
            destination: githubPath,
            commit: result.commit
        });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[Transfer Error]', error);
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message,
            stage: error.stage || 'unknown'
        });
    }
});

// POST /api/transfer/github-to-local
router.post('/github-to-local', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { githubPath, localPath } = req.body;
        
        if (!githubPath || !localPath) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Both githubPath and localPath required'
            });
        }

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'GitHub not connected'
            });
        }

        console.log(`[Transfer] Fetching from GitHub: ${githubPath}`);
        const content = await githubService.getFileContent(githubPath);
        
        console.log(`[Transfer] Writing to local: ${localPath}`);
        await filesystemService.writeFile(localPath, content);

        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'Transfer completed successfully',
            source: githubPath,
            destination: localPath
        });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[Transfer Error]', error);
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message,
            stage: error.stage || 'unknown'
        });
    }
});

// POST /api/transfer/batch - Batch transfer multiple files
router.post('/batch', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { operations } = req.body;
        
        if (!Array.isArray(operations)) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Operations array required'
            });
        }

        const results = [];
        const errors = [];

        for (let i = 0; i < operations.length; i++) {
            const op = operations[i];
            try {
                if (op.direction === 'local-to-github') {
                    const content = await filesystemService.readFile(op.source);
                    let sha = null;
                    try {
                        const info = await githubService.getFileInfo(op.destination);
                        sha = info.sha;
                    } catch (e) {}
                    
                    if (sha) {
                        await githubService.updateFile(op.destination, content, sha, op.message || `Update ${op.source}`);
                    } else {
                        await githubService.createFile(op.destination, content, op.message || `Create ${op.source}`);
                    }
                } else if (op.direction === 'github-to-local') {
                    const content = await githubService.getFileContent(op.source);
                    await filesystemService.writeFile(op.destination, content);
                }
                
                results.push({ 
                    success: true, 
                    operation: op,
                    index: i
                });
                
                // Emit progress (if using websockets, could broadcast here)
                console.log(`[Batch Transfer] Progress: ${i + 1}/${operations.length}`);
                
            } catch (err) {
                errors.push({ 
                    success: false, 
                    operation: op, 
                    error: err.message,
                    index: i
                });
            }
        }

        res.json({
            success: errors.length === 0,
            completed: results.length,
            failed: errors.length,
            total: operations.length,
            results,
            errors
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// GET /api/transfer/progress - For polling transfer progress (placeholder for future websocket implementation)
router.get('/progress', (req, res) => {
    res.json({
        success: true,
        active: false,
        progress: 0,
        message: 'No active transfer'
    });
});

module.exports = router;

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/server/services/filesystemService.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// server/services/filesystemService.js - Local Filesystem Service
const fs = require('fs').promises;
const path = require('path');

const BASE_PATH = '/';

class FilesystemService {
    constructor() {
        this.basePath = BASE_PATH;
    }

    sanitizePath(inputPath) {
        let normalized = path.normalize(inputPath);
        normalized = path.resolve(normalized);
        
        if (!normalized.startsWith('/')) {
            normalized = path.join(process.cwd(), normalized);
        }
        
        return normalized;
    }

    async listDirectory(dirPath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(dirPath);

        try {
            const entries = await fs.readdir(safePath, { withFileTypes: true });

            const files = await Promise.all(entries.map(async (entry) => {
                const fullPath = path.join(safePath, entry.name);
                const stats = await fs.stat(fullPath).catch(() => null);

                return {
                    name: entry.name,
                    type: entry.isDirectory() ? 'directory' : 'file',
                    size: stats ? stats.size : 0,
                    modified: stats ? stats.mtime.toISOString() : new Date().toISOString(),
                    permissions: stats ? stats.mode.toString(8) : 'unknown',
                    owner: stats ? stats.uid : null,
                    group: stats ? stats.gid : null
                };
            }));

            return files.sort((a, b) => {
                if (a.type === b.type) return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
                return a.type === 'directory' ? -1 : 1;
            });
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot read directory: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async getDirectoryTree(dirPath, depth = 0, maxDepth = 10) {
        if (depth > maxDepth) return null;
        
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(dirPath);
        
        try {
            const entries = await fs.readdir(safePath, { withFileTypes: true });
            const result = [];
            
            for (const entry of entries) {
                const item = {
                    name: entry.name,
                    type: entry.isDirectory() ? 'directory' : 'file'
                };
                
                if (entry.isDirectory()) {
                    const subPath = path.join(safePath, entry.name);
                    item.children = await this.getDirectoryTree(subPath, depth + 1, maxDepth);
                }
                
                result.push(item);
            }
            
            return result.sort((a, b) => {
                if (a.type === b.type) return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
                return a.type === 'directory' ? -1 : 1;
            });
        } catch (error) {
            return null;
        }
    }

    async countDirectoryContents(dirPath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(dirPath);
        
        try {
            const entries = await fs.readdir(safePath, { withFileTypes: true });
            let files = 0;
            let folders = 0;
            
            for (const entry of entries) {
                if (entry.isDirectory()) folders++;
                else files++;
            }
            
            return { files, folders };
        } catch (error) {
            return { files: 0, folders: 0 };
        }
    }

    async readFile(filePath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);

        try {
            const ext = path.extname(safePath).toLowerCase();
            const binaryExts = ['.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.gif', '.ico', '.pdf', '.zip', '.mp4', '.mp3', '.webm'];

            if (binaryExts.includes(ext)) {
                return await fs.readFile(safePath);
            }

            return await fs.readFile(safePath, 'utf-8');
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot read file: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async writeFile(filePath, content) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);

        try {
            const dir = path.dirname(safePath);
            await fs.mkdir(dir, { recursive: true });
            await fs.writeFile(safePath, content, 'utf-8');
            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot write file: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async deleteFile(filePath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);

        try {
            const stats = await fs.stat(safePath);

            if (stats.isDirectory()) {
                await fs.rmdir(safePath, { recursive: true });
            } else {
                await fs.unlink(safePath);
            }

            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot delete: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async renameFile(oldPath, newPath) {
        const safeOld = this.sanitizePath(oldPath);
        const safeNew = this.sanitizePath(newPath);

        try {
            await fs.rename(safeOld, safeNew);
            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot rename: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async createDirectory(dirPath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(dirPath);

        try {
            await fs.mkdir(safePath, { recursive: true });
            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error(`Cannot create directory: ${error.message}`);
        }
    }

    async fileExists(filePath) {
        try {
            const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);
            await fs.access(safePath);
            return true;
        } catch {
            return false;
        }
    }

    async getFileStats(filePath) {
        const safePath = this.sanitizePath(filePath);
        const stats = await fs.stat(safePath);
        const counts = stats.isDirectory() ? await this.countDirectoryContents(safePath) : { files: 0, folders: 0 };
        
        return {
            size: stats.size,
            modified: stats.mtime.toISOString(),
            created: stats.birthtime.toISOString(),
            permissions: stats.mode.toString(8),
            owner: stats.uid,
            group: stats.gid,
            isDirectory: stats.isDirectory(),
            fileCount: counts.files,
            folderCount: counts.folders
        };
    }

    async getSystemRoots() {
        return [
            { path: '/', name: 'Root Filesystem' },
            { path: '/storage/emulated/0', name: 'Internal Storage' },
            { path: '/data/data/com.termux/files/home', name: 'Termux Home' },
            { path: '/sdcard', name: 'SD Card' },
            { path: process.cwd(), name: 'Current Working Directory' }
        ];
    }
}

module.exports = new FilesystemService();

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/server/services/githubService.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// server/services/githubService.js - GitHub API Service with rename backup
const https = require('https');
const fs = require('fs').promises;
const path = require('path');

class GitHubService {
    constructor() {
        this.token = null;
        this.repo = null;
        this.owner = null;
        this.repoName = null;
        this.apiBase = 'api.github.com';
        this.branch = 'main';
        this.backupDir = path.join(process.cwd(), 'system', 'github_panel', 'renamed');
    }

    setCredentials(token, repo) {
        this.token = token;
        this.repo = repo;
        
        const parts = repo.split('/');
        if (parts.length !== 2) {
            throw new Error('Repository must be in format "owner/repo"');
        }
        this.owner = parts[0];
        this.repoName = parts[1];
    }

    isConnected() {
        return !!(this.token && this.repo && this.owner && this.repoName);
    }

    async request(apiPath, method = 'GET', data = null) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const options = {
                hostname: this.apiBase,
                path: apiPath,
                method: method,
                headers: {
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${this.token}`,
                    'Accept': 'application/vnd.github+json',
                    'User-Agent': 'MT-Git-Manager/2.0',
                    'X-GitHub-Api-Version': '2022-11-28'
                }
            };

            if (data) {
                options.headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';
            }

            const req = https.request(options, (res) => {
                let body = '';
                res.on('data', chunk => body += chunk);
                res.on('end', () => {
                    try {
                        const parsed = JSON.parse(body);
                        if (res.statusCode >= 200 && res.statusCode < 300) {
                            resolve(parsed);
                        } else {
                            reject(new Error(parsed.message || `HTTP ${res.statusCode}`));
                        }
                    } catch (e) {
                        reject(new Error('Invalid JSON response'));
                    }
                });
            });

            req.on('error', (err) => reject(err));

            if (data) {
                req.write(JSON.stringify(data));
            }
            
            req.end();
        });
    }

    async validateConnection(token, repo) {
        const prevToken = this.token;
        const prevRepo = this.repo;
        
        this.token = token;
        this.repo = repo;
        const parts = repo.split('/');
        this.owner = parts[0];
        this.repoName = parts[1];
        
        try {
            const result = await this.request(`/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}`);
            // Get default branch
            this.branch = result.default_branch || 'main';
            return result;
        } catch (error) {
            this.token = prevToken;
            this.repo = prevRepo;
            this.owner = null;
            this.repoName = null;
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async listContents(path = '') {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${path}?ref=${this.branch}`;
        const data = await this.request(url);
        
        const items = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [data];
        
        return items.map(item => ({
            name: item.name,
            type: item.type === 'dir' ? 'directory' : 'file',
            path: item.path,
            sha: item.sha,
            size: item.size || 0,
            download_url: item.download_url,
            html_url: item.html_url
        }));
    }

    async getFileContent(filePath) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${filePath}?ref=${this.branch}`;
        const data = await this.request(url);
        
        if (data.content) {
            return Buffer.from(data.content, 'base64').toString('utf-8');
        }
        
        throw new Error('No content in response');
    }

    async getFileInfo(filePath) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${filePath}?ref=${this.branch}`;
        return await this.request(url);
    }

    async getFileCommitInfo(filePath) {
        try {
            const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/commits?path=${encodeURIComponent(filePath)}&per_page=1`;
            const commits = await this.request(url);
            if (commits && commits.length > 0) {
                return {
                    date: commits[0].commit?.committer?.date,
                    author: commits[0].commit?.author?.name,
                    message: commits[0].commit?.message
                };
            }
            return null;
        } catch (err) {
            return null;
        }
    }

    async createFile(filePath, content, message) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${filePath}`;
        const encodedContent = Buffer.from(content).toString('base64');
        
        const data = {
            message: message,
            content: encodedContent,
            branch: this.branch
        };

        return await this.request(url, 'PUT', data);
    }

    async updateFile(filePath, content, sha, message) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${filePath}`;
        const encodedContent = Buffer.from(content).toString('base64');
        
        const data = {
            message: message,
            content: encodedContent,
            sha: sha,
            branch: this.branch
        };

        return await this.request(url, 'PUT', data);
    }

    async deleteFile(filePath, sha, message) {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/contents/${filePath}`;
        
        const data = {
            message: message,
            sha: sha,
            branch: this.branch
        };

        return await this.request(url, 'DELETE', data);
    }

    // Rename implementation: fetch -> create new -> delete old -> backup
    async renameFile(oldPath, newPath, sha, message) {
        console.log(`[GitHub Rename] ${oldPath} -> ${newPath}`);
        
        try {
            // Step 1: Fetch original content
            const content = await this.getFileContent(oldPath);
            const fileInfo = await this.getFileInfo(oldPath);
            
            // Step 2: Create backup
            await this.createRenameBackup(oldPath, newPath, content, fileInfo);
            
            // Step 3: Create file with new name
            const createResult = await this.createFile(
                newPath, 
                content, 
                message || `Rename ${oldPath} to ${newPath} via MT-Git Manager`
            );
            
            // Step 4: Delete original file
            const deleteResult = await this.deleteFile(
                oldPath,
                sha,
                `Delete ${oldPath} after rename to ${newPath}`
            );
            
            return {
                success: true,
                oldPath,
                newPath,
                createCommit: createResult.commit,
                deleteCommit: deleteResult.commit
            };
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('[GitHub Rename Error]', error);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async createRenameBackup(oldPath, newPath, content, fileInfo) {
        try {
            await fs.mkdir(this.backupDir, { recursive: true });
            
            const timestamp = Date.now();
            const backupId = `${timestamp}_${path.basename(oldPath)}`;
            const backupPath = path.join(this.backupDir, backupId);
            
            // Save original file content
            await fs.writeFile(`${backupPath}_old`, content, 'utf-8');
            
            // Save new file content (same at rename time)
            await fs.writeFile(`${backupPath}_new`, content, 'utf-8');
            
            // Save metadata
            const metadata = {
                oldName: path.basename(oldPath),
                newName: path.basename(newPath),
                originalPath: oldPath,
                newPath: newPath,
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                fileSize: fileInfo.size || content.length,
                branch: this.branch,
                sha: fileInfo.sha
            };
            
            await fs.writeFile(
                `${backupPath}_metadata.json`,
                JSON.stringify(metadata, null, 2)
            );
            
            console.log(`[Backup] Created backup: ${backupId}`);
            return backupId;
        } catch (err) {
            console.error('[Backup Error]', err);
            // Don't throw - backup failure shouldn't stop rename
        }
    }

    async listBranches() {
        const url = `/repos/${this.owner}/${this.repoName}/branches`;
        return await this.request(url);
    }

    setBranch(branch) {
        this.branch = branch;
    }
}

module.exports = new GitHubService();

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// server/server.js - Main entry point
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const path = require('path');
const fs = require('fs').promises;

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 8080;
const HOST = process.env.HOST || '0.0.0.0';

// Middleware
app.use(cors());
app.use(express.json({ limit: '100mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '100mb' }));

// Request logging
app.use((req, res, next) => {
    console.log(`[${new Date().toISOString()}] ${req.method} ${req.path}`);
    next();
});

// Routes
app.use('/api/local', require('./routes/localStorage'));
app.use('/api/github', require('./routes/github'));
app.use('/api/transfer', require('./routes/transfer'));

// Health check endpoint
app.get('/api/health', (req, res) => {
    res.json({ 
        status: 'ok', 
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        version: '2.0.0'
    });
});

// Server info endpoint
app.get('/api/info', (req, res) => {
    res.json({
        name: 'MT-Git Manager Server',
        version: '2.0.0',
        features: [
            'dual-panel-file-manager',
            'github-integration',
            'multi-select',
            'batch-transfer',
            'inline-rename',
            'properties-panel',
            'directory-tree',
            'smart-search'
        ]
    });
});

// Serve static client files
app.use(express.static(path.join(__dirname, '../client')));

// Fallback to index.html for SPA routes
app.get('*', (req, res) => {
    res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, '../client/index.html'));
});

// Error handling
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
    console.error('[Error]', err);
    res.status(500).json({
        success: false,
        error: err.message || 'Internal server error'
    });
});

// Ensure system directories exist
async function ensureSystemDirs() {
    const systemDir = path.join(process.cwd(), 'system');
    const renamedDir = path.join(systemDir, 'github_panel', 'renamed');
    
    try {
        await fs.mkdir(renamedDir, { recursive: true });
        console.log('[System] Ensured backup directories exist');
    } catch (err) {
        console.error('[System] Failed to create directories:', err);
    }
}

// Start server
app.listen(PORT, HOST, async () => {
    console.log('╔════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗');
    console.log('║           MT-Git Manager Server v2.0.0                 ║');
    console.log('║     Dual-Panel File Manager with GitHub Integration    ║');
    console.log('╚════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝');
    console.log(`[Server] Running at http://${HOST}:${PORT}`);
    console.log(`[API] Base URL: http://${HOST}:${PORT}/api`);
    
    await ensureSystemDirs();
});

module.exports = app;

// server/utils/pathUtils.js - Path utility functions
const path = require('path');

const BASE_PATH = '/storage/emulated/0';

module.exports = {
    sanitizePath(inputPath) {
        let resolved = path.resolve(inputPath);
        
        if (!resolved.startsWith(BASE_PATH) && !resolved.startsWith('/')) {
            throw new Error('Access denied: invalid path');
        }
        
        return resolved;
    },

    isValidPath(inputPath) {
        try {
            this.sanitizePath(inputPath);
            return true;
        } catch {
            return false;
        }
    },

    getRelativePath(absolutePath) {
        return path.relative(BASE_PATH, absolutePath);
    },

    joinPaths(...segments) {
        return path.join(...segments);
    }
};

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /storage/emulated/0/MIUI/gitm/gitm/server/utils/fileUtils.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// server/utils/fileUtils.js - File utility functions
const path = require('path');

const MIME_TYPES = {
    '.txt': 'text/plain',
    '.md': 'text/markdown',
    '.json': 'application/json',
    '.js': 'application/javascript',
    '.ts': 'application/typescript',
    '.html': 'text/html',
    '.css': 'text/css',
    '.xml': 'application/xml',
    '.yaml': 'text/yaml',
    '.yml': 'text/yaml',
    '.png': 'image/png',
    '.jpg': 'image/jpeg',
    '.jpeg': 'image/jpeg',
    '.gif': 'image/gif',
    '.svg': 'image/svg+xml',
    '.ico': 'image/x-icon',
    '.pdf': 'application/pdf',
    '.zip': 'application/zip',
    '.tar': 'application/x-tar',
    '.gz': 'application/gzip',
    '.py': 'text/x-python',
    '.java': 'text/x-java-source',
    '.c': 'text/x-c',
    '.cpp': 'text/x-c++',
    '.go': 'text/x-go',
    '.rs': 'text/x-rust'
};

module.exports = {
    getMimeType(filename) {
        const ext = path.extname(filename).toLowerCase();
        return MIME_TYPES[ext] || 'application/octet-stream';
    },

    isTextFile(filename) {
        const textTypes = ['.txt', '.md', '.json', '.js', '.ts', '.html', '.css', 
                          '.xml', '.yaml', '.yml', '.py', '.java', '.c', '.cpp',
                          '.go', '.rs', '.php', '.rb', '.swift', '.kt'];
        const ext = path.extname(filename).toLowerCase();
        return textTypes.includes(ext);
    },

    isImageFile(filename) {
        const imageTypes = ['.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.gif', '.svg', '.ico', '.bmp', '.webp'];
        const ext = path.extname(filename).toLowerCase();
        return imageTypes.includes(ext);
    },

    formatFileSize(bytes) {
        if (bytes === 0) return '0 B';
        const k = 1024;
        const sizes = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
        const i = Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k));
        return parseFloat((bytes / Math.pow(k, i)).toFixed(2)) + ' ' + sizes[i];
    },

    getFileIcon(filename, type) {
        if (type === 'directory') return 'folder';
        
        const ext = path.extname(filename).toLowerCase();
        const iconMap = {
            '.js': 'javascript',
            '.ts': 'typescript',
            '.html': 'html',
            '.css': 'css',
            '.json': 'json',
            '.md': 'markdown',
            '.py': 'python',
            '.java': 'java',
            '.png': 'image',
            '.jpg': 'image',
            '.pdf': 'pdf',
            '.zip': 'zip'
        };
        
        return iconMap[ext] || 'file';
    }
};

// server/routes/github.js - GitHub API routes
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const githubService = require('../services/githubService');

// POST /api/github/connect
router.post('/connect', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { token, repo } = req.body;
        
        if (!token || !repo) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Token and repo (owner/name) required'
            });
        }

        const repoInfo = await githubService.validateConnection(token, repo);
        githubService.setCredentials(token, repo);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            message: 'Connected to GitHub successfully',
            repo: repoInfo,
            branch: githubService.branch
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(401).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

// GET /api/github/list?path=
router.get('/list', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { path = '' } = req.query;
        
        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Not connected to GitHub. Call /connect first.'
            });
        }

        const files = await githubService.listContents(path);
        
        res.json({
            success: true,
            path: path,
            files: files
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

            });

        if (!githubService.isConnected()) {
            return res.status(401).json({

        res.json({
            success: true,
            path: path,
            content: content,
            encoding: 'utf-8'

        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });

});

                download_url: fileInfo.download_url,
                html_url: fileInfo.html_url,
                commitDate: commitInfo?.date,
                author: commitInfo?.author,
                branch: githubService.branch
            }
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Path parameter required'
            });
        }

        const content = await filesystemService.readFile(filePath);
        
        const ext = filePath.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
        const mimeTypes = {
            'txt': 'text/plain',
            'json': 'application/json',
            'js': 'application/javascript',
            'html': 'text/html',
            'css': 'text/css',
            'md': 'text/markdown'
        };
        
        res.setHeader('Content-Type', mimeTypes[ext] || 'text/plain');
        res.send(content);
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});
